
---
title: '纳米气泡可能是气泡簇！'
categories: 
 - 新媒体

<div>   
<p style="margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; line-height: 34px; background: rgb(247, 248, 250); box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;">纳米气泡是一种悖论，按照传统的物理学原理，体积越小的气泡，表面张力越大，气泡的压强越高。由于气压和气体溶解度相关，小气泡大压强导致气体越来越快溶解。这意味着纳米尺度的气泡不可能长时间存在于液体。但最近对纳米气泡的研究非常明确表明，纳米气泡可以数日稳定存在于液体。至今科学家对这种纳米气泡寿命悖论没有合理解释。最近德国学者根据研究提出一种设想，认为过去所谓100纳米大小的纳米气泡，实际上是由数百万更小的纳米气泡组成的气泡团簇。这一新发现，也许给纳米气泡的研究提供了一个新方向。</p><p style="margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; line-height: 34px; background: rgb(247, 248, 250); box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;">根据这个说法，纳米气泡在自然界中广泛存在的事实。让我们应该慎重考虑一个问题，那就是纳米气泡的生物学作用。</p><p style="margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; line-height: 34px; background: rgb(247, 248, 250); box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><br></p><p style="margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; line-height: 34px; background: rgb(247, 248, 250); box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: AdvGulliv-R; color: #000000; font-size: 16px;">氢思语：认真阅读本文后，我有一个想法。非极性气体分子如氢气氧气氮气在水中溶解度都非常小，这些溶解在水中的气体分子，和周围水分子之间存在相互排斥的作用，当然由于非常接近，也可能存在范德华力。考虑到气体溶解度非常低，例如每10万个水分子才能溶解1-2个这种气体分子，这说明相互吸引的范德华力在这里不占任何优势，而相互排斥的力相对比较强大。这种相互排斥的力就可能在气体分子周围形成一个空穴，形成空穴也就意味着形成纳米气泡。考虑到气体密度，1-2纳米的空间大概就是1-2个气体分子。这种纳米级别的气泡，难到和溶解的气体分子是一个东东，也许不是。如果不是，这种1纳米粒径的气泡可能含有比较多的气体分子。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; line-height: 34px; background: rgb(247, 248, 250); box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: AdvGulliv-R; color: #000000; font-size: 16px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; line-height: 34px; background: rgb(247, 248, 250); box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: AdvGulliv-R; color: #000000; font-size: 16px;">1前言</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; line-height: 34px; background: rgb(247, 248, 250); box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">过去</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">10</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">年中，包括我们在内的许多作者报告了悬浮在纯水中的一种新型纳米实体的存在和持久性，称为超细气泡或体相纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">(</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">本文简称</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">)</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">可以通过许多不同的物理和化学方法生成。最近，我们使用各种物理和化学技术证明，这些纳米实体确实是气泡，不能归因于任何已知形式的杂质污染。与纳米粒子类似，它们携带显著的表面负电荷，这可能是纳米气泡异常长寿的全部或部分原因。我们还阐明了添加表面活性剂、盐或</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">pH</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">调节对</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">的影响，因此，不同的表面活性剂分子</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">(</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">非离子、阴离子、阳离子</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">)</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">以不同的方式影响</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">。非离子表面活性剂不影响纳米气泡的大小分布、数量密度或表面电荷，但有望提供空间稳定的悬浮液。阴离子表面活性剂不影响纳米气泡的数密度或尺寸分布，但随着表面电荷的增加，阴离子表面活性剂可通过所谓的电</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">-</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">空间稳定机制提高纳米气泡的稳定性。另一方面，阳离子表面活性剂会逐渐使表面电位发生变化，导致纳米气泡界面电荷发生逆转，从而对纳米气泡的数密度和尺寸分布产生复杂的影响。在较低的表面活性剂浓度下，这可能会破坏悬浮液的稳定性，但在较高的浓度下，当表面电荷再次增加，超过电荷反转点时，稳定性会恢复。假设带负电荷的纳米气泡界面产生一个外部负静电压力来平衡内部拉普拉斯压力，因此，在平衡时，没有净气体扩散聚变发生。添加少量的任何价盐会导致气泡数密度的急剧减少和平均气泡大小的急剧增加。这种效应在高盐价存在时更倾向于，它归因于由共离子形成的电双层层的筛选，这降低了外部负静电压力，导致纳米气泡界面上的压力不平衡，然后膨胀。我们还认为，在纯水中，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">OH -</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">离子的吸附导致在带负电荷的</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">周围形成电双层，类似于在固体纳米粒子周围观察到的电双层。在酸性介质中，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">的不稳定归因于外部静电压力和内部拉普拉斯压力之间的平衡被破坏，这是由低</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">pH</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">值下较低的表面电位引起的。因此，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">在酸性介质中趋于不稳定和消失，而在碱性介质中稳定性增强。同样地，我们发现，当</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">悬浮在水中经过先冻结后解冻的过程时，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">会消失。上述发现最终形成了一个假设，即观察到的纳米实体不是单个纳米气泡，而是小得多的原生</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">的集群。因此，我们在此建议重温我们之前的一些工作，以验证这一假设。因此，</span><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; color: #0000FF; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">我们使用一组实验程序来表明，在纯水中观察到的典型的</span></strong><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; color: #0000FF; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">100 nm</span></strong><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; color: #0000FF; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">量级的纳米实体是一团</span></strong><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; color: #0000FF; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">1 nm</span></strong><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; color: #0000FF; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">量级的微小纳米气泡，</span></strong><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">通过演示</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">:(i)</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">当水的</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">pH</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">变为酸性时，观察到的纳米实体分解成</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">更</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">微小的</span><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; color: #0000FF; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">初级纳米气泡</span></strong><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">，当</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">pH</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">效应</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;">10%</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体;">氢氧化钾水溶液</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;">(KOH, Sigma Aldrich, UK)</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体;">中</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;">30</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体;">分钟，然后用超纯水漂洗，微波炉中干燥，用高纯干燥氮气流冲洗</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;">(BOC, UK)</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体;">实现的。在进行任何纳米尺度实体存在的实验之前，使用</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;">Nanosight</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体;">和</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;">Zetasizer</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体;">仪器对</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体;">悬浮液进行表征，对纯化水和所有缓冲溶液进行了初步检查，但未检测到显著水平的杂质。</span></span></p><p style="margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; line-height: 34px; background: rgb(247, 248, 250); box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">2</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial;">.</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">2. </span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;">纳米气泡</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Arial; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 16px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; line-height: 34px; background: rgb(247, 248, 250); box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px;
